 Facebook company whatsapp has taken a big step to deal with fake news and rumors
 haalanki company ne isaki shuruyaat pehle hi kii thi
 Actually whatsapp imposed a limit on forwarding the message last year
 ek baar main 20 indiviual yaa group main ek yujar watsap massej forward kar saktaa tha
 But now the company has reduced its limit
 ab ek yujar sirf paanch massej forward kar saktaa he
 Interestingly, the update designed to forward messages to 5 users had arrived in India only in July last year
 lekin ab company ne is feechar ko global banane kaa elaan kiya he
 That is, whatsapp users around the world will also be able to forward whatsapp messages to only five people at a time
 royatres kii ek report ke mutabik watsap kii policy and communication vaais president victoria grand ne kaha he, â€˜aaj se duniya bhar ke watsap yugers ke liye watsap massej forward karne kii limit ko gata kar 5 kiya ja rahaa heâ€™
 Company officials have said that whatsapp Message Forward can be confined to fight misinformation and rumors
 gauratlab he ki phek news or afvaahon ko rokane ke lievotsapane forward kiye gaye massej main label dene shuru kiya he
 Apart from this, people are being asked to stop fake news and rumors through advertisements on Indian newspaper and TV
 phek news or afvaahon ke alaava aaj kal watsap child pornography ke lekar bhi news main he
 The company has deleted 1 lakh 30 thousand accounts in this sequence
 iske liye company ne artificial intelligence tul kii madad lee he or avaidh activity ke shaq par acounts delit kiye gaye hai
 a report by an Israeli NGO said that in India too, there are hundreds of groups active in the name of child pornography and objectionable videos are shared
 watsap ke mutabik company aise maamalon par jiro tolerance policy rakhti he or isse nipatane ke liye sabase advanced technolji kaa yuj kiya ja rahaa he
 These technology profiles scan photos and descriptions and those accounts are banned on suspicion of being associated with child pornography
 chunki watsap ke chats and tu and ancrypted hote hai or aisi sthiti main sender or resiver ke alaava koi doosraa chat nahin pard saktaa he
 So the company cannot see chat content
 company ne is tarah ke acounts hataane ke liye artificial intelligence besd tul taiyaar kiya he
 There is a wave of outrage in the country after former Indian Navy Kulbhushan Jadhav was sentenced to death in Pakistan
 pakistan ne kulbhushan jadhav ko ro kaa agent bataate hue pakistan main jasusi kaa aarope lagaaya he
 Spying has been happening around the world for hundreds of years
 puraane jamaane main raja-maharaaja apane dushmano kii jasusi karavaate the
 In the new era, every country has set up intelligence agencies for spying, whose job is to spy on the government, political party or important person
 aaie jaanate hai duniya kii top 5 khufia agenciyon ke bare main
 
 
 1- India's RAW India's intelligence agency RAW i
e
 Research and Analysis Wing has been considered as the world's strongest intelligence agency
 isaki sthapana 1968 main kii gai thi
 It is headquartered in Delhi
 is agency kii khaasiyat yah he ki bharat ke pradhanmantri ke alaava kisi ke prati javabdeh nahin he
 RAW keeps complete information about foreign affairs, criminals, terrorists
 vahiin, intelligence beuro (ibi) bhi desh kii suraksha ke liye kaam karti he
 The two agencies together have foiled many major terrorist attacks
 2- pakistan kii isipakiswana kii khufia agency iesai yani inter services intelegence ko duniya kii number ek khufia agency mana jaataa he
 It was established in the year 1948
 iskaa mukhyalay islamabad ke shahrah e soharavardi main he
 It was founded by Major General R
, a British Army officer of Australian descent
 cathom ne rakhi thi, jo us vakt pakistani army staff ke mukhya the
 ISI is accused of promoting terrorism in the name of protecting the country
 kai aatanki hamalon main uskaa haath mana jaataa he
 3- America's CIA America's intelligence agency CIA i
e
 Central Intelligence Agency was established in the year 1947
 iskaa mukhyalay washington ke paas varjeenia main he
 The CIA is considered the most capable and powerful in the world, not just America
 siie ke alaava america main teen agenciyaan enese, diie or epabiai hai
 The cia's job is to collect information from abroad including cybercrime, counter terrorism
 2013 main washington post ne siie ko sabase zyada bajet vaali khufia agency bataaya tha
 4- Israel's MOSSAD Israel's intelligence agency Mossad is counted among the world's best and most dangerous intelligence agencies
 isaki sthapana saal 1949 kii gai thi
 Its director reports directly to the Prime Minister
 mosaad kaa matlab maut mana jaataa he
 It is said that once one stepped into the eyes of Mossad, it is difficult to escape
 mosaad ke khoonkhaar agent use duniya ke kisi bhi kone se dhund nikaalane kaa dam rakhte hai
 Mossad has access to every place where any conspiracy is being hatched against Israel or its citizens
 5- china kaa msscina kii khufia agency emesas yani ministry of state sicurity sabase badi khufia agency he
 It was established in 1983
 iskaa mukhyalay bijing main he
 Its work is also like the intelligence agency of the rest of the countries, but it works to protect the country politically

 It has been said by a section in the country that if Sardar Patel had been the first Prime Minister of the country, this would have happened
 yah alag baat he ki sardaar patel piem banate bhi to aazaadee ke mahaj teen saal baad tak hi rah pate, kyonki 1950 main unka nidhan ho gaya tha
 But was there ever a situation for Patel to become PM? Could he be PM? a clear answer to this question is that as long as Nehru was in Congress, it could not happen
 kya he isaki vajah aaie jaanate hai
 How India got British rule had become very weak after the First World War II
 1946 main british sarkaar ne cabinet mishan plan banaaya, jiske tahat kuch angrej adhikariyon ko ye jimmedaari mili ki ve bharat kii aazaadee ke liye bhartiya netaaon se baat karen
 It was decided that an interim government will be formed in India
 antarim sarkaar ke taur par vysarai kii ekjicutive council banani thi
 The British Viceroy was to be its President, while the President of the Congress Party was to become the Vice President of this Council
 aage chalakar aazaadee ke baad isi vaais president kaa pradhanmantri bananaa lagbhag tay tha
 At that time, Maulana Abul Kalam Azad was the President of the Congress Party
 kai bade netaaon ke jail main rahane kii vajah se vah is pad par 1940 se hi bane hue the
 Maulana Azad did not want to leave the post at this time, but under pressure from Mahatma Gandhi, he agreed to step down and then started the search for the next president of Congress who would also become the first Prime Minister of India
 ise bhi padhein: kya mahatma gandhi kii hatya ke liye aresas ko jimmedaar maanate the sardaar patel?yah tay karne ke liye april 1946 main congress kaarysmiti kii baithak bulaai gai
 Many big Congress leaders including Mahatma Gandhi, Nehru, Sardar Patel, Acharya Kripalani, Rajendra Prasad, Khan Abdul Ghaffar Khan were present in this meeting
 mahatma gandhi pandit nehru ko congress kaa adhyaksh bananaa chaahate the
 He was a popular mass leader, but had fewer people supporting him in the provincial committees of the Congress
 15 main se 12 prantiy samitiyon ne sardaar patel ke naam kaa samarthan kiyabaithak main tab party ke mahasachiv acharya je bi kriplani ne kaha â€˜baapu ye parpanra rahi he ki congress adhyaksh pad kaa chunaav prantiy congress cametiyaan karti hai, kisi bhi prantiy congress cameti ne jawahar laal nehru kaa naam adhyaksh pad ke liye prastaavit nahin kiya he
 Of the 15, 12 Provincial Congress Committees have proposed the name of Sardar Patel and the remaining 3 committees have named Mera and Pattabhi Sitaramaiya
 ' iskaa yah saaf matlab tha ki congress adhyaksh pad ke liye sardaar patel ke paas bahumat tha, vahiin jawahar laal nehru kaa naam hi prastaavit nahin tha
 Nehru's name came under pressure from Mahatma Gandhi, but Mahatma Gandhi wanted to see Jawaharlal Nehru as the Prime Minister of India
 is ahm baithak se kuch din pehle hi gandhi ne moulana ko likhaa tha, 'agar mujhase poocha jaae to main jawahar laal ko hi praathamikta duungaa
 i have many reasons for this
 'mahatma gandhi ke is rukh ke baavjood 1946 ke april maheene main congress kaarysmiti kii baithak main charchaa ke liye bhi jawahar laal nehru kaa naam prastaavit nahin hua

 saudi arab ke moulanaon (dharmaguruon) kii ghani dadhi ke bare main micro-bloging website twitor par likhte vakt soad al-shaimari ne sochaa bhi nahin tha ki uske vichaar use jailyatra karvaa sakate hai, lekin hua vahi
 
 
 Divorced 42-year-old Soad al-shamari, who spoke about women's rights, posted pictures of several bearded men, including a traditionalist Jew, a hippie, a communist, a Turkish caliph, a Sikh, and a Muslim
 
 
 soad al-shaimari ne in tasveeron ke saath likhaa ki sirf dadhi rakh lene se koi vyakti pavitra yaa muslim nahin ho jaataa
 
 
 He also pointed out that during the time of Prophet Mohammad, one of the most staunch critics of Islam had a longer beard than the Prophet
 
 
 islamic kanoon main snaatak kii degree hasil kar chuki chah bacchon kii maa soad al-shaimari ke liye is tarah kii bebaak tippaniyan karnaa koi nai baat nahin he
 
 
 Born into a religious family of a large clan, Soad may have grazed sheep as a child, but is now a liberal activist demanding women's rights, and often challenging the powerful religious authority of Saudi Arabia with his arguments about Islam 
 
 
 apane vichaaron kii soad ko keemat bhi chukaani padi he
 
 
 She has spent three months in jail without any formal charge 'for instigating public sentiments'
 
 
 sarkaar unki videsh yatraaon par pabandi laga chuki he
 
 
 His online forum 'free Saudi Liberals Network' co-founder and blogger Raf Badawi is serving a 10-year prison sentence, and he was also publicly lobbied for 50 lashes
 
 
 soad ke pita saarvajanik rup se unhen beti sweekaar karne se inkaar kar chuke hai
 
 
 But all this was not enough to suppress the voice of Soad al-shaimri
 
 
 soad al-shaimari kahati hai, "mere paas kuch adhikaar hai, jo mere hisaab se mere dharm ke khilaaf nahin hai
 
 
 i want to demand those rights, and want those who make decisions, listen to me and then do something
 
 
 " Women Islamic scholars and activists in Arab countries have long demanded a fresh interpretation of Sharia laws that give equal status to men and women in front of God
 
 
 soad al-shaimari kaa shumaar saudi arab main sabase zyaada awaz uthaane vaali tathaa sakriy dharmik tathaa mahila adhikaron kii pairokaron main kiya jaataa he
 
 
 Sohad Nasif, a friend and fellow activist of Soad, says, "he (soad al-shamri) has complete confidence in what he says, and he is not hesitant at all
 
 
 vah arab prishthbhumi se hai, registani maahaul se
 
 
 She is proud of her background, but due to this background she becomes somewhat dry with everyone, and is very dry expressing her views
 
 
 " Raised as the eldest of 12 children of a farmer in the Haile province, Soad al-shaymari cared for the sheep
 
 
 vah na sirf dharmik thim, balki 'salaafi' (aisa musalmaan, jo islamic kanoonon kii shabdic vyakhya ko jyon kaa tyon sweekaar karata or maanata he) ke rup main rahati thim
 
 
 Soad al-shamari became a public school teacher after earning a bachelor's degree in Islamic law from the University of Haile
 
 
 17 saal kii umr main soad ne apane hi kabeeley ke apane se doguni umr ke purush se shaadi kii thi, or phir ek beti - yaara - bhi hui
 
 
 Soad got divorced at the age of 20, and they remarried
 
 
 soad kii duusari shaadi hil ke usee chif jaj se hui, jisane unke talaak ke maamle ko dekha tha
 
 
 After this, the war of rights for Soad al-shamri began on the day his daughter was snatched from him
 
 
 jaise hi yaara saat baras kii hui, soad ke pehle pati ko uski castady saunp di gai
 
 
 Since Soad had remarried, the court ruled that the girl should stay with her father instead of living with another man
 
 
 soad al-shaimari kahati hai, "jab unhone use (yaara ko) mujhase liya, or kaha 'yahi allaah kii marzi he' or 'yahi islam he', thik usee vakt mere andar vidroh kii chingaari sulag uthi
 
 
 It is not possible that there is such a God in the world, who will tolerate this injustice and suffering just because i am a woman
 
 
 " She could not even see her daughter, so for eight years she fought with her parents, her community and everyone who came between her and her daughter Yara
 
 
 bhavaheen chehre ke saath haath baandhe baat karti hui soad al-shaimari kahati hai, "main pagal-si ho rahi thi, lekin apane mata-pita ke saamne, apane jaj pati ke saamne, or unke aasapaas maujuud hamaare samudaay ke logon ke saamne, mere naam or samudaay main meri jagah kii vajah se mujhase ummid kii jaati thi ki main chupchaap baithi sab kuch dekhati rahun
 
 
 " duusari shaadi se soad al-shaimari ko paanch santaanen huin, lekin uske baad jald hi uskaa phir talaak ho gaya
 
 
 When Yara's father became ill, and his grandmother passed away, Yara's father, who was 16 years old, finally allowed him to live with his mother, and Soad al-shaimri was more lenient with all six of his children
 The visiting cities settled in Jeddah
 
 
 sharia kanoon kii apni jaankaree ko soad ne zaruuratmand auraton kii kanoonee salaahkaar (legal adwiser) ke rup main istemaal kiya
 
 
 Sometimes his advice was less pious, more full of treachery and shamelessness
 
 
 ek baar unhone apni ek mitra ko salaah di ki vah pataa kare ki uske cese ko koun-sa jaj dekh rahaa he, phir kuch mechap kare, or jaj ke saamne ro-rokar taarikh aage badhaane kaa aagrah kare
